'''Write a function to convert rgb color to hsv color. https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/program-change-rgb-color-model-hsv-color-model/'''
def rgb_to_hsv(r, g, b):
    r = int(r)
    g = int(g)
    b = int(b)
    if r == 0 and g == 0 and b == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif r == 0 and g == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif r == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif g == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif b == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif r == 255:
        return 255, 255, 255
    elif g == 255:
        return 255, 255, 255
    elif b == 255:
        return 255, 255, 255
    elif r == 0 or g == 0 or b == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif r == 0 or g == 0 or b == 0:
        return 0

'''Write a function to convert rgb color to hsv color. https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/program-change-rgb-color-model-hsv-color-model/'''
def rgb_to_hsv(r, g, b):
    r = int(r)
    g = int(g)
    b = int(b)
    if r == 0 and g == 0 and b == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif r == 0 and g == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif r == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif g == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif b == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif r == 255:
        return 255, 255, 255
    elif g == 255:
        return 255, 255, 255
    elif b == 255:
        return 255, 255, 255
    elif r == 0 or g == 0 or b == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif r == 0 or g == 0 or b == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif r == 0 or g == 0:
        return 0,

'''Write a function to convert rgb color to hsv color. https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/program-change-rgb-color-model-hsv-color-model/'''
def rgb_to_hsv(r, g, b):
    r = int(r)
    g = int(g)
    b = int(b)
    if r == 0 and g == 0 and b == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif r == 0 and g == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif r == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif g == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif b == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif r == 255:
        return 255, 255, 255
    elif g == 255:
        return 255, 255, 255
    elif b == 255:
        return 255, 255, 255
    elif r == 0 or g == 0 or b == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif r == 0 or g == 0 or b == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif r == 0 or g == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
    elif r == 0:
        return 0, 0, 0
